    219 +fn Value* matrix_singular_values_try_cuda_value(TensorVal* matrix, Interp* interp) {

    258 +fn Value* matrix_norm_try_cuda_value(TensorVal* matrix, MatrixNormKind kind, Interp* interp) {
    259 +    if (matrix == null || matrix.device != TENSOR_DEVICE_CUDA) return null;
    260 +    if (kind != MATRIX_NORM_SPECTRAL && kind != MATRIX_NORM_NUCLEAR) return null;
    261 +    if (!tensor_dtype_is_fixed_complex(matrix.dtype)) {
    262 +        return raise_error_with_payload_names(interp, "tensor", "tensor/backend-unsupported", "matrix/norm: CUDA currently supports Complex128 or Complex64 spectr

    263 +    }
    264 +    if (matrix.rank != 2 || matrix.shape == null) {

    281 +    if (status != OMNI_TENSOR_CUDA_SUCCESS) {
    282 +        return tensor_cuda_status_raise(interp, status, "matrix/norm: CUDA cuSOLVER SVD failed");
    283 +    }
    284 +    if (k == 0) return make_double(interp, 0.0);
    285 +    if (s_device == null) return tensor_runtime_raise(interp, "matrix/norm: CUDA cuSOLVER SVD did not return singular value storage");
    286 +    double norm = 0.0;
    287 +    if (matrix.dtype == TENSOR_DTYPE_COMPLEX128) {
    288 +        double* s_host = null;
    289 +        if (!matrix_double_workspace_zero(k, &s_host)) {

    296 +        }

    298 +        if (status != OMNI_TENSOR_CUDA_SUCCESS) {

    300 +        }

    303 +        } else {

    305 +        }

    315 +        }

      1 +#include <math.h>
      2 +#include <stddef.h>
      3 +
      4 +extern "C" __global__ void omni_cuda_ml_sgd_f32(
      5 +    const float* params,
      6 +    const float* grads,
      7 +    const float* velocity,
      8 +    float learning_rate,
      9 +    float momentum,
     10 +    float weight_decay,
     11 +    unsigned int has_velocity,
     12 +    size_t element_count,
     13 +    float* out_params,
     14 +    float* out_velocity
     15 +) {
     16 +    size_t idx = (size_t)blockIdx.x * (size_t)blockDim.x + (size_t)threadIdx.x;
     17 +    if (idx >= element_count) return;
     18 +
     19 +    float param_value = params[idx];
     20 +    float effective_grad = grads[idx] + weight_decay * param_value;
     21 +    if (momentum > 0.0f) {
     22 +        float next_velocity = effective_grad;
     23 +        if (has_velocity != 0u) next_velocity += momentum * velocity[idx];
     24 +        if (out_velocity != NULL) out_velocity[idx] = next_velocity;
     25 +        out_params[idx] = param_value - learning_rate * next_velocity;
     26 +        return;
     27 +    }
     28 +    out_params[idx] = param_value - learning_rate * effective_grad;
     29 +}
     30 +
     31 +extern "C" __global__ void omni_cuda_ml_adam_f32(
     32 +    const float* params,
     33 +    const float* grads,
     34 +    const float* first,
     35 +    const float* second,
     36 +    float learning_rate,
     37 +    float beta1,
     38 +    float beta2,
     39 +    float epsilon,
     40 +    float weight_decay,
     41 +    float first_correction,
     42 +    float second_correction,
     43 +    unsigned int decoupled_weight_decay,
     44 +    unsigned int has_moments,
     45 +    size_t element_count,
     46 +    float* out_params,
     47 +    float* out_first,
     48 +    float* out_second
     49 +) {
     50 +    size_t idx = (size_t)blockIdx.x * (size_t)blockDim.x + (size_t)threadIdx.x;
     51 +    if (idx >= element_count) return;
     52 +
     53 +    float param_value = params[idx];
     54 +    float grad_value = grads[idx];
     55 +    float moment_grad = decoupled_weight_decay != 0u ? grad_value : grad_value + weight_decay * param_value;
     56 +    float old_first = has_moments != 0u ? first[idx] : 0.0f;
     57 +    float old_second = has_moments != 0u ? second[idx] : 0.0f;
     58 +    float next_first = beta1 * old_first + (1.0f - beta1) * moment_grad;
     59 +    float next_second = beta2 * old_second + (1.0f - beta2) * moment_grad * moment_grad;
     60 +    float first_hat = next_first / first_correction;
     61 +    float second_hat = next_second / second_correction;
     62 +    float decay_update = decoupled_weight_decay != 0u ? learning_rate * weight_decay * param_value : 0.0f;
     63 +
     64 +    out_params[idx] = param_value - decay_update - (learning_rate * first_hat / (sqrtf(second_hat) + epsilon));
     65 +    out_first[idx] = next_first;
     66 +    out_second[idx] = next_second;
     67 +}
     68 +
     69 +extern "C" __global__ void omni_cuda_ml_rmsprop_f32(
     70 +    const float* params,
     71 +    const float* grads,
     72 +    const float* square,
     73 +    const float* velocity,
     74 +    float learning_rate,
     75 +    float alpha,
     76 +    float epsilon,
     77 +    float momentum,
     78 +    float weight_decay,
     79 +    unsigned int has_square,
     80 +    unsigned int has_velocity,
     81 +    size_t element_count,
     82 +    float* out_params,
     83 +    float* out_square,
     84 +    float* out_velocity
     85 +) {
     86 +    size_t idx = (size_t)blockIdx.x * (size_t)blockDim.x + (size_t)threadIdx.x;
     87 +    if (idx >= element_count) return;
     88 +
     89 +    float param_value = params[idx];
     90 +    float effective_grad = grads[idx] + weight_decay * param_value;
     91 +    float old_square = has_square != 0u ? square[idx] : 0.0f;
     92 +    float next_square = alpha * old_square + (1.0f - alpha) * effective_grad * effective_grad;
     93 +    float scaled_update = learning_rate * effective_grad / (sqrtf(next_square) + epsilon);
     94 +    out_square[idx] = next_square;
     95 +
     96 +    if (momentum > 0.0f) {
     97 +        float old_velocity = has_velocity != 0u ? velocity[idx] : 0.0f;
     98 +        float next_velocity = momentum * old_velocity + scaled_update;
     99 +        if (out_velocity != NULL) out_velocity[idx] = next_velocity;
    100 +        out_params[idx] = param_value - next_velocity;
    101 +        return;
    102 +    }
    103 +    out_params[idx] = param_value - scaled_update;
    104 +}

• Added scripts/run_vulkan_math_perf_probe.sh (+98 -0)
     1 +#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2 +set -euo pipefail
     3 +
     4 +cd "$(dirname "$0")/.."
     5 +
     6 +: "${OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_BUILD:=0}"
     7 +: "${OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_LOG:=build/vulkan_math_perf_probe.log}"
     8 +: "${OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_TIMEOUT:=45s}"
     9 +
    10 +if [[ "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_BUILD" == "1" ]]; then
    11 +  source scripts/c3c_limits.sh
    12 +  omni_c3 build --obj-out obj
    13 +fi
    14 +
    15 +mkdir -p "$(dirname "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_LOG")"
    16 +: > "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_LOG"
    17 +
    18 +runtime_ld_library_path="${LD_LIBRARY_PATH:-/usr/local/lib}"
    19 +if [[ -n "${OMNI_DOCKER_TOOLCHAIN_ROOT:-}" ]]; then
    20 +  runtime_ld_library_path="/opt/omni-host-toolchain/lib"
    21 +fi
    22 +
    23 +extract_elapsed_ms() {
    24 +  sed -n 's/^\[\([0-9][0-9]*\).*/\1/p' <<< "$1"
    25 +}
    26 +
    27 +normalize_output() {
    28 +  tr ' ' ',' <<< "$1"
    29 +}
    30 +
    31 +run_probe() {
    32 +  local suite="$1"
    33 +  local label="$2"
    34 +  local dtype="$3"
    35 +  local n="$4"
    36 +  local expr="$5"
    37 +  local out
    38 +  local ms
    39 +  local normalized
    40 +
    41 +  echo "=== Vulkan Math Perf Probe: ${label} ===" | tee -a "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_LOG"
    42 +  out="$(timeout "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_TIMEOUT" env LD_LIBRARY_PATH="$runtime_ld_library_path" ./build/main --eval "$expr")"
    43 +  echo "$out" | tee -a "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_LOG"
    44 +
    45 +  if [[ "$out" == "skip" ]]; then
    46 +    echo "OMNI_BENCH_SUMMARY suite=${suite} label=${label} dtype=${dtype} n=${n} available=0" \
    47 +      | tee -a "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_LOG"
    48 +    return 0
    49 +  fi
    50 +
    51 +  ms="$(extract_elapsed_ms "$out")"
    52 +  if [[ -z "$ms" ]]; then
    53 +    echo "FAIL: ${label} did not produce a timed array result: ${out}" >&2
    54 +    return 1
    55 +  fi
    56 +
    57 +  normalized="$(normalize_output "$out")"
    58 +  echo "OMNI_BENCH_SUMMARY suite=${suite} label=${label} dtype=${dtype} n=${n} available=1 ms=${ms} result=${normalized}" \
    59 +    | tee -a "$OMNI_VULKAN_MATH_PERF_LOG"
    60 +}
    61 +
    62 +svd_expr() {
    63 +  local dtype="$1"
    64 +  local n="$2"
    65 +  local matrix_expr="$3"
    66 +  cat <<EOF
    67 +(let (b (ref (tensor-backends) 3)) (if (ref b '$(tr '[:upper:]' '[:lower:]' <<< "$dtype")) (let (start (time-ms) s (to-device (matrix/singular-values (to-device ${matrix_expr} 'vulkan)) 'cpu) finish (time-ms)) (Array (- fi
        nish start) (length s) (ref s [0]) (ref s [$(("$n" - 1))]))) 'skip))
    68 +EOF
    69 +}
    70 +
    71 +eigen_expr() {
    72 +  local capability="$1"
    73 +  local n="$2"
    74 +  local matrix_expr="$3"
    75 +  cat <<EOF
    76 +(let (b (ref (tensor-backends) 3)) (if (ref b '${capability}) (let (start (time-ms) e (to-device (matrix/eigenvalues (to-device ${matrix_expr} 'vulkan)) 'cpu) finish (time-ms)) (Array (- finish start) (length e) (ref e [0]
        ) (ref e [$(("$n" - 1))]))) 'skip))
    77 +EOF
    78 +}
    79 +
    80 +run_probe "vulkan_math_svd" "f64_identity_64" "Float64" "64" \
    81 +  "$(svd_expr "Float64" "64" "(matrix/identity 64 Float64)")"
    82 +run_probe "vulkan_math_svd" "f64_identity_65" "Float64" "65" \
    83 +  "$(svd_expr "Float64" "65" "(matrix/identity 65 Float64)")"
    84 +run_probe "vulkan_math_svd" "f64_ones_65" "Float64" "65" \
    85 +  "$(svd_expr "Float64" "65" "(Tensor Float64 [65 65] 1.0)")"
    86 +run_probe "vulkan_math_svd" "f64_zero_65" "Float64" "65" \
    87 +  "$(svd_expr "Float64" "65" "(Tensor Float64 [65 65] 0.0)")"
    88 +run_probe "vulkan_math_svd" "f32_identity_65" "Float32" "65" \
    89 +  "$(svd_expr "Float32" "65" "(matrix/identity 65 Float32)")"
    90 +
    91 +run_probe "vulkan_math_eigen" "f64_identity_64" "Float64" "64" \
    92 +  "$(eigen_expr "float64" "64" "(matrix/identity 64 Float64)")"
    93 +run_probe "vulkan_math_eigen" "f64_identity_65" "Float64" "65" \
    94 +  "$(eigen_expr "float64" "65" "(matrix/identity 65 Float64)")"
    95 +run_probe "vulkan_math_eigen" "f64_ones_65" "Float64" "65" \
    96 +  "$(eigen_expr "float64" "65" "(Tensor Float64 [65 65] 1.0)")"
    97 +run_probe "vulkan_math_eigen" "c64_zero_65" "Complex64" "65" \
    98 +  "$(eigen_expr "complex64" "65" "(Tensor Complex64 [65 65] 0)")"

    14 +
    15 +The script runs small capability-gated Vulkan fixtures and emits

    17 +`time-ms` primitive inside the runtime process, so startup time is excluded
    18 +from the reported `ms` field. The script intentionally covers the 64/65
    19 +storage-backed threshold and representative diagonal, zero, and rank-deficient

    73 +    if (tensor == null || !tensor_has_valid_metadata(tensor)) return false;
    74 +    if (tensor.storage_offset != 0) return false;
    75 +    if (tensor.rank == 0) return tensor.storage_element_count >= tensor.element_count;

    77 +
    78 +    usz max_offset = 0;
    79 +    for (usz axis = 0; axis < tensor.rank; axis++) {
    80 +        usz dim = tensor.shape[axis];
    81 +        if (dim == 0) return true;
    82 +        usz extent = dim - 1;
    83 +        usz axis_offset = 0;
    84 +        if (!tensor_checked_mul_usz(extent, tensor.strides[axis], &axis_offset)) return false;
    85 +        if (axis_offset > usz.max - max_offset) return false;
    86 +        max_offset += axis_offset;
    87 +    }
    88 +    return max_offset < tensor.storage_element_count;

─ Worked for 1m 42s ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• These advanced failures share one root cause: the JIT tail-position shortcut for List and Array treats a single argument as a variadic element, bypassing the real constructor/conversion primitive. That skips proper-list and

• Edited docs/plans/vulkan-eigensolver-plan-2026-04-17.md (+82 -0)
    148
    149 +## General Complex Vulkan Design Boundary
    150 +
    151 +Decision recorded 2026-04-22 for
    152 +`TENSOR-100H-COMPLEX-EIGEN-VULKAN-GENERAL`: do not ship a 2x2-only or
    153 +triangular-only shortcut as the next step. The native Vulkan route must target
    154 +one shared non-Hermitian solver boundary for `Complex128` and `Complex64`.
    155 +
    156 +Chosen solver family:
    157 +
    158 +- staged complex Hessenberg reduction plus implicit shifted QR;
    159 +- right-eigenvector back-accumulation from the same transformations used by the
    160 +  Schur/eigenvalue iteration;
    161 +- final per-eigenvalue vector refinement/residual check before public routing.
    162 +
    163 +Rejected/deferred families:
    164 +
    165 +- direct dense QR without Hessenberg reduction: too weak as the shared boundary
    166 +  because it spends unnecessary work per iteration and gives poor convergence
    167 +  control for clustered spectra;
    168 +- realification of complex matrices: invalid as the primary contract because it
    169 +  loses the direct complex eigenpair pairing semantics already rejected in TODO
    170 +  and memory;
    171 +- Hermitian Jacobi reuse: only valid for Hermitian inputs and already shipped
    172 +  under `matrix/eigenvalues` / `matrix/eigenvectors`, not general
    173 +  `matrix/eigenpairs`;
    174 +- hidden CPU/LAPACK fallback: prohibited for Vulkan operands.
    175 +
    176 +Helper ABI target:
    177 +
    178 +- `omni_tensor_backend_vulkan_general_eigen_complex128(input, byte_len, n,
    179 +  &out_values, &out_vectors)` and the matching `complex64` helper;
    180 +- output `values` is a Vulkan `Complex128`/`Complex64` rank-1 tensor with `n`
    181 +  complex elements;
    182 +- output `vectors` is a Vulkan `Complex128`/`Complex64` rank-2 tensor with
    183 +  shape `[n n]`, columns aligned with `values`;
    184 +- the C helper owns all scratch/status buffers and returns only public output
    185 +  handles on success;
    186 +- status slots must distinguish invalid shape/byte length, unsupported resource
    187 +  bounds, non-convergence, and allocation/dispatch failure;
    188 +- helper validation must reject `n*n` and byte-count overflow, `n > UINT32_MAX`,
    189 +  and any scratch size that cannot be represented in Vulkan descriptor ranges.
    190 +
    191 +Scratch layout target:
    192 +
    193 +- matrix workspace `H` in complex component storage, initialized from input;
    194 +- accumulated right-vector matrix `Q`, initialized to identity and updated by
    195 +  the same Householder/Givens transformations as `H`;
    196 +- per-column Householder/vector scratch and per-step shift/status scratch;
    197 +- private status buffer for convergence, deflation count, and first failing
    198 +  iteration;
    199 +- no public output buffer may contain status sentinels. Unlike symmetric
    200 +  eigenvalues, general complex values are a dense complex tensor and status must
    201 +  live in a private buffer that is read and destroyed before success returns.
    202 +
    203 +Implementation sub-boundaries:
    204 +
    205 +1. Add helper ABI declarations and fail-closed C entry points with validation,
    206 +   no shader routing, and no capability flip.
    207 +2. Add checked-in GLSL/SPIR-V for a serial correctness-first prototype covering
    208 +   small dense matrices through the same ABI, with private status and output
    209 +   buffers. This may be one invocation/workgroup, but it must be the same
    210 +   Hessenberg/QR boundary, not a special case.
    211 +3. Add C3 routing only after residual tests pass for both `Complex128` and
    212 +   `Complex64`, `tensor-backends` capability bits reflect helper availability,
    213 +   and LAPACK `zgeev`/`cgeev` counters prove no CPU fallback for Vulkan inputs.
    214 +4. Treat larger staged/multi-dispatch performance as a follow-up only after the
    215 +   correctness-first native ABI is green.
    216 +
    217 +Validation additions required before capability bits flip:
    218 +
    219 +- Vulkan `Complex128` and `Complex64` `matrix/eigenpairs` values/vectors remain
    220 +  Vulkan-placed with result dtype matching CPU fixed-width contract;
    221 +- residual checks validate `A * v ~= lambda * v` after explicit CPU copyback;
    222 +- triangular, diagonal, non-normal, repeated-value, and non-Hermitian examples;
    223 +- no hidden CPU/LAPACK fallback: `zgeev` and `cgeev` counters unchanged for
    224 +  Vulkan inputs;
    225 +- unsupported layout/view/mixed-device inputs fail closed before helper
    226 +  dispatch;
    227 +- shader compile, `spirv-val`, helper rebuild, `c3c build --obj-out obj`,
    228 +  focused host and bounded-container `advanced-collections-module`, file-size
    229 +  gate, and status consistency gate.
    230 +
    231  ## Deferred Boundaries

• I’ve got the route plan: use the vector output buffer with extra private scratch, keep values public-sized, and use a private status output. The shader will run a serial shifted complex QR iteration, reconstruct right
  eigenvectors from the triangular Schur form, sort by the existing public ordering, and fail closed on non-convergence.

     39 +bool is_finite_f64(double value) {
     40 +    return value == value && (value - value) == 0.0lf;
     41 +}
     42 +
     43 +Complex c_make(double real, double imag) {
     44 +    Complex out_value;
     45 +    out_value.real = real;
     46 +    out_value.imag = imag;
     47 +    return out_value;
     48 +}
     49 +
     50 +Complex c_add(Complex left, Complex right) {
     51 +    return c_make(left.real + right.real, left.imag + right.imag);
     52 +}
     53 +
     54 +Complex c_sub(Complex left, Complex right) {
     55 +    return c_make(left.real - right.real, left.imag - right.imag);
     56 +}
     57 +
     58 +Complex c_scale(Complex value, double scale) {
     59 +    return c_make(value.real * scale, value.imag * scale);
     60 +}
     61 +
     62 +Complex c_mul(Complex left, Complex right) {
     63 +    return c_make(
     64 +        left.real * right.real - left.imag * right.imag,
     65 +        left.real * right.imag + left.imag * right.real
     66 +    );
     67 +}
     68 +
     69 +Complex c_conj(Complex value) {
     70 +    return c_make(value.real, -value.imag);
     71 +}
     72 +
     73 +double c_abs_squared(Complex value) {
     74 +    return value.real * value.real + value.imag * value.imag;
     75 +}
     76 +
     77 +bool c_finite(Complex value) {
     78 +    return is_finite_f64(value.real) && is_finite_f64(value.imag);
     79 +}
     80 +
     81 +Complex c_div(Complex numerator, Complex denominator) {
     82 +    double denom = c_abs_squared(denominator);
     83 +    if (!(denom > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f64(denom)) {
     84 +        return c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf);
     85 +    }
     86 +    return c_scale(c_mul(numerator, c_conj(denominator)), 1.0lf / denom);
     87 +}

     89 +uint scalar_index(uint complex_base, uint row, uint col) {
     90 +    return 2u * (complex_base + row * pc.n + col);
     91 +}

     93 +Complex matrix_get(uint complex_base, uint row, uint col) {
     94 +    uint index = scalar_index(complex_base, row, col);
     95 +    return c_make(eigen_vectors[index], eigen_vectors[index + 1u]);
     96 +}

     98 +void matrix_set(uint complex_base, uint row, uint col, Complex value) {

    100 +    eigen_vectors[index] = value.real;
    101 +    eigen_vectors[index + 1u] = value.imag;
    102 +}

    123 +    }

    126 +    }

    128 +}

    131 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    132 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    133 +            matrix_set(base, row, col, c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf));
    134 +        }

    136 +    return true;

    139 +bool initialize_state(uint public_base, uint a_base) {
    140 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    141 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    142 +            Complex value = input_at(row, col);
    143 +            if (!c_finite(value)) return false;
    144 +            matrix_set(a_base, row, col, value);
    145 +            matrix_set(public_base, row, col, row == col ? c_make(1.0lf, 0.0lf) : c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf));
    146 +        }
    147 +    }
    148 +    return true;
    149 +}
    150 +
    151 +bool qr_decompose(uint a_base, uint q_base, uint r_base, Complex shift) {
    152 +    clear_matrix(q_base);
    153 +    clear_matrix(r_base);
    154 +    for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    155 +        for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    156 +            Complex value = matrix_get(a_base, row, col);
    157 +            if (row == col) value = c_sub(value, shift);
    158 +            matrix_set(q_base, row, col, value);
    159 +        }
    160 +        for (uint prev = 0u; prev < col; prev++) {
    161 +            Complex dot = c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf);
    162 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    163 +                dot = c_add(dot, c_mul(c_conj(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev)), matrix_get(q_base, row, col)));
    164 +            }
    165 +            if (!c_finite(dot)) return false;
    166 +            matrix_set(r_base, prev, col, dot);
    167 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    168 +                Complex reduced = c_sub(matrix_get(q_base, row, col), c_mul(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev), dot));
    169 +                if (!c_finite(reduced)) return false;
    170 +                matrix_set(q_base, row, col, reduced);
    171 +            }
    172 +        }
    173 +        double norm_squared = 0.0lf;
    174 +        for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    175 +            norm_squared += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(q_base, row, col));
    176 +        }
    177 +        if (!(norm_squared > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f64(norm_squared)) {
    178 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    179 +                matrix_set(q_base, row, col, row == col ? c_make(1.0lf, 0.0lf) : c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf));
    180 +            }
    181 +            for (uint prev = 0u; prev < col; prev++) {
    182 +                Complex dot = c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf);
    183 +                for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    184 +                    dot = c_add(dot, c_mul(c_conj(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev)), matrix_get(q_base, row, col)));
    185 +                }
    186 +                for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    187 +                    matrix_set(q_base, row, col, c_sub(matrix_get(q_base, row, col), c_mul(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev), dot)));
    188 +                }
    189 +            }
    190 +            norm_squared = 0.0lf;
    191 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    192 +                norm_squared += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(q_base, row, col));
    193 +            }
    194 +        }
    195 +        if (!(norm_squared > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f64(norm_squared)) {
    196 +            return false;
    197 +        }
    198 +        double inv_norm = 1.0lf / sqrt(norm_squared);
    199 +        if (!is_finite_f64(inv_norm)) return false;
    200 +        matrix_set(r_base, col, col, c_make(sqrt(norm_squared), 0.0lf));
    201 +        for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    202 +            matrix_set(q_base, row, col, c_scale(matrix_get(q_base, row, col), inv_norm));
    203 +        }
    204 +    }
    205 +    return true;
    206 +}
    207 +
    208 +bool multiply(uint left_base, uint right_base, uint out_base) {
    209 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    210 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    211 +            Complex sum = c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf);
    212 +            for (uint k = 0u; k < pc.n; k++) {
    213 +                sum = c_add(sum, c_mul(matrix_get(left_base, row, k), matrix_get(right_base, k, col)));
    214 +            }
    215 +            if (!c_finite(sum)) return false;
    216 +            matrix_set(out_base, row, col, sum);
    217 +        }
    218 +    }
    219 +    return true;
    220 +}
    221 +
    222 +bool copy_matrix(uint source_base, uint target_base) {
    223 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    224 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    225 +            matrix_set(target_base, row, col, matrix_get(source_base, row, col));
    226 +        }
    227 +    }
    228 +    return true;
    229 +}

    231 +double lower_offdiag_norm(uint a_base) {
    232 +    double sum = 0.0lf;
    233 +    for (uint row = 1u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    234 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < row; col++) {
    235 +            sum += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(a_base, row, col));
    236 +        }
    237 +    }
    238 +    return sum;
    239 +}
    240 +
    241 +double matrix_norm(uint a_base) {
    242 +    double sum = 0.0lf;
    243 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    244 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    245 +            sum += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(a_base, row, col));
    246 +        }
    247 +    }
    248 +    return sum;
    249 +}
    250 +
    251 +bool solve_eigenvector(uint a_base, uint accum_base, uint y_base, uint out_col, Complex lambda) {
    252 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    253 +        matrix_set(y_base, row, 0u, c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf));
    254 +    }
    255 +    matrix_set(y_base, out_col, 0u, c_make(1.0lf, 0.0lf));
    256 +    for (uint step = 0u; step < out_col; step++) {
    257 +        uint row = out_col - 1u - step;
    258 +        Complex sum = c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf);
    259 +        for (uint col = row + 1u; col <= out_col; col++) {
    260 +            sum = c_add(sum, c_mul(matrix_get(a_base, row, col), matrix_get(y_base, col, 0u)));
    261 +        }
    262 +        Complex denom = c_sub(matrix_get(a_base, row, row), lambda);
    263 +        Complex value = c_abs_squared(denom) > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS
    264 +            ? c_scale(c_div(sum, denom), -1.0lf)
    265 +            : c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf);
    266 +        if (!c_finite(value)) return false;
    267 +        matrix_set(y_base, row, 0u, value);
    268 +    }
    269 +    double norm_squared = 0.0lf;
    270 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    271 +        Complex sum = c_make(0.0lf, 0.0lf);
    272 +        for (uint k = 0u; k < pc.n; k++) {
    273 +            sum = c_add(sum, c_mul(matrix_get(accum_base, row, k), matrix_get(y_base, k, 0u)));
    274 +        }
    275 +        if (!c_finite(sum)) return false;
    276 +        matrix_set(0u, row, out_col, sum);
    277 +        norm_squared += c_abs_squared(sum);
    278 +    }
    279 +    if (!(norm_squared > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f64(norm_squared)) return false;
    280 +    double inv_norm = 1.0lf / sqrt(norm_squared);
    281 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    282 +        matrix_set(0u, row, out_col, c_scale(matrix_get(0u, row, out_col), inv_norm));
    283 +    }
    284 +    return true;
    285 +}
    286 +
    287 +void phase_normalize_column(uint col) {
    288 +    uint pivot_row = 0u;
    289 +    double pivot_abs = 0.0lf;
    290 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    291 +        double candidate = c_abs_squared(matrix_get(0u, row, col));
    292 +        if (candidate > pivot_abs) {
    293 +            pivot_abs = candidate;
    294 +            pivot_row = row;
    295 +        }
    296 +    }
    297 +    if (!(pivot_abs > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS)) return;
    298 +    Complex anchor = matrix_get(0u, pivot_row, col);
    299 +    Complex phase = c_scale(c_conj(anchor), 1.0lf / sqrt(pivot_abs));
    300 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    301 +        matrix_set(0u, row, col, c_mul(matrix_get(0u, row, col), phase));
    302 +    }
    303 +}
    304 +
    305 +bool eigen_precedes(uint left, uint right) {
    306 +    Complex lv = value_get(left);
    307 +    Complex rv = value_get(right);
    308 +    double lm = c_abs_squared(lv);
    309 +    double rm = c_abs_squared(rv);
    310 +    if (lm > rm) return true;
    311 +    if (lm < rm) return false;
    312 +    if (lv.real > rv.real) return true;
    313 +    if (lv.real < rv.real) return false;
    314 +    return lv.imag > rv.imag;
    315 +}
    316 +
    317 +void swap_columns(uint left, uint right) {
    318 +    Complex tmp_value = value_get(left);
    319 +    value_set(left, value_get(right));
    320 +    value_set(right, tmp_value);
    321 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    322 +        Complex tmp = matrix_get(0u, row, left);
    323 +        matrix_set(0u, row, left, matrix_get(0u, row, right));
    324 +        matrix_set(0u, row, right, tmp);
    325 +    }
    326 +}
    327 +
    328 +void sort_eigenpairs() {
    329 +    for (uint i = 0u; i < pc.n; i++) {
    330 +        uint best = i;
    331 +        for (uint j = i + 1u; j < pc.n; j++) {
    332 +            if (eigen_precedes(j, best)) best = j;
    333 +        }
    334 +        if (best != i) swap_columns(i, best);
    335 +    }
    336 +}
    337 +
    338 +void main() {
    339 +    if (gl_GlobalInvocationID.x != 0u) return;
    340 +    if (pc.value_count < pc.n || pc.vector_count < pc.n * pc.n ||
    341 +        pc.vector_storage_count < 5u * pc.vector_count) {
    342 +        return;
    343 +    }
    344 +    zero_outputs();
    345 +    if (pc.n == 0u) {
    346 +        status_values[0] = 0.0lf;
    347 +        return;
    348 +    }
    349 +
    350 +    uint public_base = 0u;
    351 +    uint a_base = pc.vector_count;
    352 +    uint q_base = 2u * pc.vector_count;
    353 +    uint r_base = 3u * pc.vector_count;
    354 +    uint tmp_base = 4u * pc.vector_count;
    355 +
    356 +    if (!initialize_state(public_base, a_base)) {
    357 +        status_values[0] = 1.0lf;
    358 +        return;
    359 +    }
    360 +
    361 +    bool converged = lower_offdiag_norm(a_base) <= OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * (matrix_norm(a_base) + 1.0lf);
    362 +    for (uint iteration = 0u; iteration < pc.max_iterations && !converged; iteration++) {
    363 +        Complex shift = matrix_get(a_base, pc.n - 1u, pc.n - 1u);
    364 +        if (!qr_decompose(a_base, q_base, r_base, shift)) {
    365 +            status_values[0] = 2.0lf;
    366 +            return;
    367 +        }
    368 +        if (!multiply(r_base, q_base, tmp_base)) {
    369 +            status_values[0] = 1.0lf;
    370 +            return;
    371 +        }
    372 +        for (uint i = 0u; i < pc.n; i++) {
    373 +            matrix_set(tmp_base, i, i, c_add(matrix_get(tmp_base, i, i), shift));
    374 +        }
    375 +        if (!multiply(public_base, q_base, r_base)) {
    376 +            status_values[0] = 1.0lf;
    377 +            return;
    378 +        }
    379 +        copy_matrix(r_base, public_base);
    380 +        copy_matrix(tmp_base, a_base);
    381 +        converged = lower_offdiag_norm(a_base) <= OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * (matrix_norm(a_base) + 1.0lf);
    382 +    }
    383 +    if (!converged) {
    384 +        status_values[0] = 2.0lf;
    385 +        return;
    386 +    }
    387 +
    388 +    for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    389 +        Complex lambda = matrix_get(a_base, col, col);
    390 +        value_set(col, lambda);
    391 +        if (!solve_eigenvector(a_base, public_base, r_base, col, lambda)) {
    392 +            status_values[0] = 2.0lf;
    393 +            return;
    394 +        }
    395 +        phase_normalize_column(col);
    396 +    }
    397 +    sort_eigenpairs();
    398 +    status_values[0] = 0.0lf;
    399 +}

     38 +bool is_finite_f32(float value) {
     39 +    return value == value && (value - value) == 0.0;
     40 +}
     41 +
     42 +Complex c_make(float real, float imag) {
     43 +    Complex out_value;
     44 +    out_value.real = real;
     45 +    out_value.imag = imag;
     46 +    return out_value;
     47 +}
     48 +
     49 +Complex c_add(Complex left, Complex right) {
     50 +    return c_make(left.real + right.real, left.imag + right.imag);
     51 +}
     52 +
     53 +Complex c_sub(Complex left, Complex right) {
     54 +    return c_make(left.real - right.real, left.imag - right.imag);
     55 +}
     56 +
     57 +Complex c_scale(Complex value, float scale) {
     58 +    return c_make(value.real * scale, value.imag * scale);
     59 +}
     60 +
     61 +Complex c_mul(Complex left, Complex right) {
     62 +    return c_make(
     63 +        left.real * right.real - left.imag * right.imag,
     64 +        left.real * right.imag + left.imag * right.real
     65 +    );
     66 +}
     67 +
     68 +Complex c_conj(Complex value) {
     69 +    return c_make(value.real, -value.imag);
     70 +}
     71 +
     72 +float c_abs_squared(Complex value) {
     73 +    return value.real * value.real + value.imag * value.imag;
     74 +}
     75 +
     76 +bool c_finite(Complex value) {
     77 +    return is_finite_f32(value.real) && is_finite_f32(value.imag);
     78 +}
     79 +
     80 +Complex c_div(Complex numerator, Complex denominator) {
     81 +    float denom = c_abs_squared(denominator);
     82 +    if (!(denom > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f32(denom)) {
     83 +        return c_make(0.0, 0.0);
     84 +    }
     85 +    return c_scale(c_mul(numerator, c_conj(denominator)), 1.0 / denom);
     86 +}
     87 +
     88 +uint scalar_index(uint complex_base, uint row, uint col) {
     89 +    return 2u * (complex_base + row * pc.n + col);
     90 +}
     91 +
     92 +Complex matrix_get(uint complex_base, uint row, uint col) {
     93 +    uint index = scalar_index(complex_base, row, col);
     94 +    return c_make(eigen_vectors[index], eigen_vectors[index + 1u]);
     95 +}
     96 +
     97 +void matrix_set(uint complex_base, uint row, uint col, Complex value) {
     98 +    uint index = scalar_index(complex_base, row, col);
     99 +    eigen_vectors[index] = value.real;
    100 +    eigen_vectors[index + 1u] = value.imag;
    101 +}
    102 +
    103 +Complex input_at(uint row, uint col) {
    104 +    uint index = 2u * (row * pc.n + col);
    105 +    return c_make(input_values[index], input_values[index + 1u]);
    106 +}
    107 +
    108 +Complex value_get(uint col) {
    109 +    uint index = 2u * col;
    110 +    return c_make(eigen_values[index], eigen_values[index + 1u]);
    111 +}
    112 +
    113 +void value_set(uint col, Complex value) {
    114 +    uint index = 2u * col;
    115 +    eigen_values[index] = value.real;
    116 +    eigen_values[index + 1u] = value.imag;
    117 +}
    118 +
    119 +void zero_outputs() {
    120 +    for (uint index = 0u; index < 2u * pc.value_count; index++) {
    121 +        eigen_values[index] = 0.0;
    122 +    }
    123 +    for (uint index = 0u; index < 2u * pc.vector_storage_count; index++) {
    124 +        eigen_vectors[index] = 0.0;
    125 +    }
    126 +    status_values[0] = 1.0;
    127 +}
    128 +
    129 +bool clear_matrix(uint base) {
    130 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    131 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    132 +            matrix_set(base, row, col, c_make(0.0, 0.0));
    133 +        }
    134 +    }
    135 +    return true;
    136 +}
    137 +
    138 +bool initialize_state(uint public_base, uint a_base) {
    139 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    140 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    141 +            Complex value = input_at(row, col);
    142 +            if (!c_finite(value)) return false;
    143 +            matrix_set(a_base, row, col, value);
    144 +            matrix_set(public_base, row, col, row == col ? c_make(1.0, 0.0) : c_make(0.0, 0.0));
    145 +        }
    146 +    }
    147 +    return true;
    148 +}
    149 +
    150 +bool qr_decompose(uint a_base, uint q_base, uint r_base, Complex shift) {
    151 +    clear_matrix(q_base);
    152 +    clear_matrix(r_base);
    153 +    for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    154 +        for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    155 +            Complex value = matrix_get(a_base, row, col);
    156 +            if (row == col) value = c_sub(value, shift);
    157 +            matrix_set(q_base, row, col, value);
    158 +        }
    159 +        for (uint prev = 0u; prev < col; prev++) {
    160 +            Complex dot = c_make(0.0, 0.0);
    161 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    162 +                dot = c_add(dot, c_mul(c_conj(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev)), matrix_get(q_base, row, col)));
    163 +            }
    164 +            if (!c_finite(dot)) return false;
    165 +            matrix_set(r_base, prev, col, dot);
    166 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    167 +                Complex reduced = c_sub(matrix_get(q_base, row, col), c_mul(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev), dot));
    168 +                if (!c_finite(reduced)) return false;
    169 +                matrix_set(q_base, row, col, reduced);
    170 +            }
    171 +        }
    172 +        float norm_squared = 0.0;
    173 +        for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    174 +            norm_squared += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(q_base, row, col));
    175 +        }
    176 +        if (!(norm_squared > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f32(norm_squared)) {
    177 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    178 +                matrix_set(q_base, row, col, row == col ? c_make(1.0, 0.0) : c_make(0.0, 0.0));
    179 +            }
    180 +            for (uint prev = 0u; prev < col; prev++) {
    181 +                Complex dot = c_make(0.0, 0.0);
    182 +                for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    183 +                    dot = c_add(dot, c_mul(c_conj(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev)), matrix_get(q_base, row, col)));
    184 +                }
    185 +                for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    186 +                    matrix_set(q_base, row, col, c_sub(matrix_get(q_base, row, col), c_mul(matrix_get(q_base, row, prev), dot)));
    187 +                }
    188 +            }
    189 +            norm_squared = 0.0;
    190 +            for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    191 +                norm_squared += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(q_base, row, col));
    192 +            }
    193 +        }
    194 +        if (!(norm_squared > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f32(norm_squared)) {
    195 +            return false;
    196 +        }
    197 +        float inv_norm = 1.0 / sqrt(norm_squared);
    198 +        if (!is_finite_f32(inv_norm)) return false;
    199 +        matrix_set(r_base, col, col, c_make(sqrt(norm_squared), 0.0));
    200 +        for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    201 +            matrix_set(q_base, row, col, c_scale(matrix_get(q_base, row, col), inv_norm));
    202 +        }
    203 +    }
    204 +    return true;
    205 +}
    206 +
    207 +bool multiply(uint left_base, uint right_base, uint out_base) {
    208 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    209 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    210 +            Complex sum = c_make(0.0, 0.0);
    211 +            for (uint k = 0u; k < pc.n; k++) {
    212 +                sum = c_add(sum, c_mul(matrix_get(left_base, row, k), matrix_get(right_base, k, col)));
    213 +            }
    214 +            if (!c_finite(sum)) return false;
    215 +            matrix_set(out_base, row, col, sum);
    216 +        }
    217 +    }
    218 +    return true;
    219 +}
    220 +
    221 +bool copy_matrix(uint source_base, uint target_base) {
    222 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    223 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    224 +            matrix_set(target_base, row, col, matrix_get(source_base, row, col));
    225 +        }
    226 +    }
    227 +    return true;
    228 +}
    229 +
    230 +float lower_offdiag_norm(uint a_base) {
    231 +    float sum = 0.0;
    232 +    for (uint row = 1u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    233 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < row; col++) {
    234 +            sum += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(a_base, row, col));
    235 +        }
    236 +    }
    237 +    return sum;
    238 +}
    239 +
    240 +float matrix_norm(uint a_base) {
    241 +    float sum = 0.0;
    242 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    243 +        for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    244 +            sum += c_abs_squared(matrix_get(a_base, row, col));
    245 +        }
    246 +    }
    247 +    return sum;
    248 +}
    249 +
    250 +bool solve_eigenvector(uint a_base, uint accum_base, uint y_base, uint out_col, Complex lambda) {
    251 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    252 +        matrix_set(y_base, row, 0u, c_make(0.0, 0.0));
    253 +    }
    254 +    matrix_set(y_base, out_col, 0u, c_make(1.0, 0.0));
    255 +    for (uint step = 0u; step < out_col; step++) {
    256 +        uint row = out_col - 1u - step;
    257 +        Complex sum = c_make(0.0, 0.0);
    258 +        for (uint col = row + 1u; col <= out_col; col++) {
    259 +            sum = c_add(sum, c_mul(matrix_get(a_base, row, col), matrix_get(y_base, col, 0u)));
    260 +        }
    261 +        Complex denom = c_sub(matrix_get(a_base, row, row), lambda);
    262 +        Complex value = c_abs_squared(denom) > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS
    263 +            ? c_scale(c_div(sum, denom), -1.0)
    264 +            : c_make(0.0, 0.0);
    265 +        if (!c_finite(value)) return false;
    266 +        matrix_set(y_base, row, 0u, value);
    267 +    }
    268 +    float norm_squared = 0.0;
    269 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    270 +        Complex sum = c_make(0.0, 0.0);
    271 +        for (uint k = 0u; k < pc.n; k++) {
    272 +            sum = c_add(sum, c_mul(matrix_get(accum_base, row, k), matrix_get(y_base, k, 0u)));
    273 +        }
    274 +        if (!c_finite(sum)) return false;
    275 +        matrix_set(0u, row, out_col, sum);
    276 +        norm_squared += c_abs_squared(sum);
    277 +    }
    278 +    if (!(norm_squared > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS) || !is_finite_f32(norm_squared)) return false;
    279 +    float inv_norm = 1.0 / sqrt(norm_squared);
    280 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    281 +        matrix_set(0u, row, out_col, c_scale(matrix_get(0u, row, out_col), inv_norm));
    282 +    }
    283 +    return true;
    284 +}
    285 +
    286 +void phase_normalize_column(uint col) {
    287 +    uint pivot_row = 0u;
    288 +    float pivot_abs = 0.0;
    289 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    290 +        float candidate = c_abs_squared(matrix_get(0u, row, col));
    291 +        if (candidate > pivot_abs) {
    292 +            pivot_abs = candidate;
    293 +            pivot_row = row;
    294 +        }
    295 +    }
    296 +    if (!(pivot_abs > OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_NORM_EPS)) return;
    297 +    Complex anchor = matrix_get(0u, pivot_row, col);
    298 +    Complex phase = c_scale(c_conj(anchor), 1.0 / sqrt(pivot_abs));
    299 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    300 +        matrix_set(0u, row, col, c_mul(matrix_get(0u, row, col), phase));
    301 +    }
    302 +}
    303 +
    304 +bool eigen_precedes(uint left, uint right) {
    305 +    Complex lv = value_get(left);
    306 +    Complex rv = value_get(right);
    307 +    float lm = c_abs_squared(lv);
    308 +    float rm = c_abs_squared(rv);
    309 +    if (lm > rm) return true;
    310 +    if (lm < rm) return false;
    311 +    if (lv.real > rv.real) return true;
    312 +    if (lv.real < rv.real) return false;
    313 +    return lv.imag > rv.imag;
    314 +}
    315 +
    316 +void swap_columns(uint left, uint right) {
    317 +    Complex tmp_value = value_get(left);
    318 +    value_set(left, value_get(right));
    319 +    value_set(right, tmp_value);
    320 +    for (uint row = 0u; row < pc.n; row++) {
    321 +        Complex tmp = matrix_get(0u, row, left);
    322 +        matrix_set(0u, row, left, matrix_get(0u, row, right));
    323 +        matrix_set(0u, row, right, tmp);
    324 +    }
    325 +}
    326 +
    327 +void sort_eigenpairs() {
    328 +    for (uint i = 0u; i < pc.n; i++) {
    329 +        uint best = i;
    330 +        for (uint j = i + 1u; j < pc.n; j++) {
    331 +            if (eigen_precedes(j, best)) best = j;
    332 +        }
    333 +        if (best != i) swap_columns(i, best);
    334 +    }
    335 +}
    336 +
    337 +void main() {
    338 +    if (gl_GlobalInvocationID.x != 0u) return;
    339 +    if (pc.value_count < pc.n || pc.vector_count < pc.n * pc.n ||
    340 +        pc.vector_storage_count < 5u * pc.vector_count) {
    341 +        return;
    342 +    }
    343 +    zero_outputs();
    344 +    if (pc.n == 0u) {
    345 +        status_values[0] = 0.0;
    346 +        return;
    347 +    }
    348 +
    349 +    uint public_base = 0u;
    350 +    uint a_base = pc.vector_count;
    351 +    uint q_base = 2u * pc.vector_count;
    352 +    uint r_base = 3u * pc.vector_count;
    353 +    uint tmp_base = 4u * pc.vector_count;
    354 +
    355 +    if (!initialize_state(public_base, a_base)) {
    356 +        status_values[0] = 1.0;
    357 +        return;
    358 +    }
    359 +
    360 +    bool converged = lower_offdiag_norm(a_base) <= OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * (matrix_norm(a_base) + 1.0);
    361 +    for (uint iteration = 0u; iteration < pc.max_iterations && !converged; iteration++) {
    362 +        Complex shift = matrix_get(a_base, pc.n - 1u, pc.n - 1u);
    363 +        if (!qr_decompose(a_base, q_base, r_base, shift)) {
    364 +            status_values[0] = 2.0;
    365 +            return;
    366 +        }
    367 +        if (!multiply(r_base, q_base, tmp_base)) {
    368 +            status_values[0] = 1.0;
    369 +            return;
    370 +        }
    371 +        for (uint i = 0u; i < pc.n; i++) {
    372 +            matrix_set(tmp_base, i, i, c_add(matrix_get(tmp_base, i, i), shift));
    373 +        }
    374 +        if (!multiply(public_base, q_base, r_base)) {
    375 +            status_values[0] = 1.0;
    376 +            return;
    377 +        }
    378 +        copy_matrix(r_base, public_base);
    379 +        copy_matrix(tmp_base, a_base);
    380 +        converged = lower_offdiag_norm(a_base) <= OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * OMNI_GENERAL_EIGEN_EPS * (matrix_norm(a_base) + 1.0);
    381 +    }
    382 +    if (!converged) {
    383 +        status_values[0] = 2.0;
    384 +        return;
    385 +    }
    386 +
    387 +    for (uint col = 0u; col < pc.n; col++) {
    388 +        Complex lambda = matrix_get(a_base, col, col);
    389 +        value_set(col, lambda);
    390 +        if (!solve_eigenvector(a_base, public_base, r_base, col, lambda)) {
    391 +            status_values[0] = 2.0;
    392 +            return;
    393 +        }
    394 +        phase_normalize_column(col);
    395 +    }
    396 +    sort_eigenpairs();
    397 +    status_values[0] = 0.0;
    398 +}

• The C helper layer now compiles syntactically. I’m adding the C3 route for Vulkan Complex128/Complex64 matrix/eigenpairs; it will still fail closed on unsupported dtype/shape/layout/status, and it will reject successful non-
  empty helper calls that return null device handles.

• Context compacted

─ Worked for 2m 10s ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• Findings

  1. Critical: ffi-callback handles segfault when released through the public foreign-release path.
     src/lisp/prim_ffi_callback.c3:207 defines ffi_callback_context_finalizer(void* raw) and casts raw to FfiCallbackContext*. But the handle is created with ctx.code_ptr as the stored FFI handle pointer at src/lisp/
     prim_ffi_callback.c3:408, while the actual ctx is only passed to libffi closure prep at src/lisp/prim_ffi_callback.c3:390. The comment at src/lisp/prim_ffi_callback.c3:424 says the context pointer is stored, but the code
     stores ctx.code_ptr.
     The release path in src/lisp/value_constructors.c3:178 passes box.lib_handle into the finalizer, and src/lisp/foreign_runtime_core.c3:360 exposes that through foreign-release. That means the finalizer receives executable
     callback code memory, not the context object, then dereferences it as a struct.
     I reproduced this with:

     LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/usr/local/lib ./build/main --eval "(let (cb (ffi-callback (lambda (a b) (+ a b)) ['Integer 'Integer] 'Integer)) (foreign-release cb))"
     Result: Segmentation fault, exit status 139. Existing tests at src/lisp/tests_advanced_io_effect_ffi_ffi_surface_groups.c3:590 cover callback creation/invocation, but not callback release.
     Result: Segmentation fault, exit status 139. Existing tests at src/lisp/tests_advanced_io_effect_ffi_ffi_surface_groups.c3:590 cover callback creation/invocation, but not callback release.
  2. High: the structured error model is documented as complete, but many public/runtime paths still emit raw string errors.
     docs/ERROR_MODEL.md:1 says the baseline is complete and defines canonical error payloads with code, message, domain, and data. The runtime has structured helpers at src/lisp/value_constructors.c3:515, but the raw raise_error
     path at src/lisp/value_constructors.c3:556 still produces a payload-less pending error.
     Static scan results in src/lisp show 1244 uses of raise_error_with_payload_names, but also 1013 non-test return raise_error(interp, ...) sites. Examples include FFI callbacks at src/lisp/prim_ffi_callback.c3:254, foreign
     runtime release/unwrap paths at src/lisp/foreign_runtime_core.c3:362, HTTP at src/lisp/http.c3:24, JSON at src/lisp/json.c3:116, and generic collection mutation at src/lisp/prim_collection_generic_set.c3:9.
     This is exactly the “sane error messages” gap: the system has the structured mechanism, but the migration is not complete enough for users or tooling to rely on it.
  3. High: ML autograd Vulkan status is internally contradictory between spec, TODO, and code.
     The language spec still says ml/grad keeps CUDA/Vulkan backward fail-closed at docs/LANGUAGE_SPEC.part-01b.md:394. But TODO records shipped Vulkan backward slices for MSE, map expressions, broadcast map, and softmax cross
     entropy at docs/todo_parts/todo_part_14.md:690. The code implements Vulkan MSE backward at src/lisp/prim_ml_autograd_tensor_expr.c3:300 and Vulkan softmax-CE backward at src/lisp/prim_ml_autograd_tensor_expr.c3:749.
     There is also a stale rejection message at src/lisp/prim_ml_autograd_tensor_expr.c3:116 that still says Vulkan backward kernels are not implemented. Current behavior may be partially correct, but the user-facing contract is
     not coherent.
  4. Medium: ML visualization/graphics tooling is not a first-class surface.
     I found generic terminal graph helpers in examples/libraries/ftxui/ui_nodes.omni:55 and example references to ui.graph, but no obvious ML-facing visualization primitives such as ml/plot, tensor image display, dataset preview,
     training curves, confusion matrices, feature map inspection, or graph/export helpers. Given the repo’s ML/tensor ambitions, this is a real product gap rather than just missing examples.
  5. Medium: validation status can mask memory/lifetime diagnostics.
     The current status consistency check reports validation green, but existing project memory records that memory-lifetime-smoke can emit boundary graph-audit violations while still reporting pass=237 fail=0. I did not rerun the
     heavy memory-lifetime suite because repo policy requires bounded container execution for those runs. The risk is that diagnostic output is not always promoted to a failing verification signal, so “green” can overstate memory-
     management health unless logs are audited or the harness is tightened.
  6. Low/Medium: bounded C-string scanning is inconsistent.
     There are hardened bounded helpers, for example src/entry_runtime_project_paths.c3:9, but several CLI/bindgen/runtime-adjacent paths still scan until NUL without a cap. Examples include src/entry_cli_helpers.c3:15, src/
     entry_bind_paths.c3:7, src/entry_bind_dep_generation.c3:371, and src/main_repl_shared.c3:21.
     This is not automatically exploitable for normal argv/env strings, but the hardening style is uneven around host/runtime boundaries.
  7. Low: exhaustive tagged-switch discipline is not enforced.
     The style guide prefers exhaustive switch handling for tagged unions such as ValueTag, but default: remains common in src/lisp. Some are likely legitimate, but examples like src/lisp/value_print.c3:104, src/lisp/
     eval_promotion_copy.c3:120, src/lisp/prim_tensor_storage.c3:29, and src/lisp/foreign_runtime_core.c3:92 should be audited so new value tags cannot silently fall into generic behavior.

  Important Stale Items Avoided

  There is an existing AUDIT_REPORT_2026-04-22.md in the dirty working tree, but I did not treat it as authoritative. Several serious items in that report appear already remediated on disk: the JIT allocation checks in src/lisp/
  jit_compile_expr_core.c3:94, REPL protocol send diagnostics in src/lisp/eval_repl_server_worker.c3:18, environment hash-table error logging in src/lisp/value_environment.c3:49, and the runtime manifest entries in src/
  entry_build_runtime_manifest_lisp_part3.c3:1.
